# AGENTS.md

## гғӘгғқгӮёгғҲгғӘжҰӮиҰҒ

- еҚҳдёҖHTMLгғ»гӮӘгғ•гғ©гӮӨгғіеӢ•дҪңгғ»и»ҪйҮҸдҫқеӯҳгҒ®гӮўгғ—гғӘзҫӨ

## гғҮгӮЈгғ¬гӮҜгғҲгғӘж§ӢжҲҗ

- `apps/<app-name>/` - гӮўгғ—гғӘ
- `apps/<app-name>/build/build.ts` - гғ“гғ«гғү
- `apps/<app-name>/generated/` - гғ“гғ«гғүеҮәеҠӣе…Ҳ
- `apps/<app-name>/src/` - гӮҪгғјгӮ№гӮігғјгғү
- `apps/<app-name>/tests/` - гғҶгӮ№гғҲ

## й–Ӣзҷәз”ЁгӮ№гӮҜгғӘгғ—гғҲ

- `npm run precommit` - гғ•гӮ©гғјгғһгғғгғҲ & еһӢгғҒгӮ§гғғгӮҜ & гғҰгғӢгғғгғҲгғҶгӮ№гғҲ & гӮӨгғігғҶгӮ°гғ¬гғјгӮ·гғ§гғігғҶгӮ№гғҲ & гғ“гғ«гғү & E2EгғҶгӮ№гғҲ & гӮҪгғјгӮ№гӮігғјгғүгғҶгӮӯгӮ№гғҲзөҗеҗҲ

## е…ұйҖҡиҰҸзҙ„

- гғ‘гӮ№гҒҢйҖҡгҒЈгҒҰгҒ„гҒӘгҒ„е ҙеҗҲгҒҜжЁ©йҷҗжҳҮж јгҒ§е®ҹиЎҢ
- дәӢеүҚиЁҲз”»гҒ«еҗ«гҒҫгӮҢгҒӘгҒ„й–ўж•°гҒ®еӨүжӣҙгҒҜзө¶еҜҫгҒ«иЎҢгӮҸгҒӘгҒ„

## гӮҪгғјгӮ№гӮігғјгғүе…ұйҖҡиҰҸзҙ„

- ж—Ҙжң¬иӘһгҒ§гӮігғЎгғігғҲиЁҳиҝ°
- DOM гҒ«еҜҫеҝңгҒҷгӮӢгӮігғјгғүгҒҜ DOM й ҶгҒ«гҖҒд»–гҒҜгҒҷгҒ№гҒҰгӮўгғ«гғ•гӮЎгғҷгғғгғҲй ҶгҒ«дёҰгҒ№гӮӢ

## TypeScript

- е…Ёй–ўж•°гҒ®иӘ¬жҳҺгӮ’ JSDoc гҒ§иЁҳиҝ°
- дёҰгҒій ҶгҒ®зӢ¬иҮӘгғ«гғјгғ«
  1. зҙ”зІӢгғӯгӮёгғғгӮҜ / гғ–гғ©гӮҰгӮ¶еүҜдҪңз”ЁпјҲйқһDOMпјү / DOM/UI гҒ®й ҶгҒ«гӮ°гғ«гғјгғ—еҢ–
  2. type / const / function гҒ®й ҶгҒ«гӮ°гғ«гғјгғ—еҢ–
  3. е…ұйҖҡгҒ®дёҰгҒій ҶгҒ«дёҰгҒ№гӮӢ

## гғҶгӮ№гғҲгӮігғјгғүе…ұйҖҡиҰҸзҙ„

- гғҶгӮ№гғҲгҒ§гҒҚгҒӘгҒ„й–ўж•°гҒҜз©әе®ҹиЈ…гҒ§гӮігғЎгғігғҲгӮўгӮҰгғҲгҒҷгӮӢ

FILE: apps/random-picker/build/build.ts
================================================
import fs from "node:fs";
import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url";
import * as prettier from "prettier";
import { build } from "esbuild";

const sourceHtmlPath = fileURLToPath(
  new URL("../src/index.html", import.meta.url),
);
const sourceCssPath = fileURLToPath(
  new URL("../src/style.css", import.meta.url),
);
const sourceScriptPath = fileURLToPath(
  new URL("../src/script.ts", import.meta.url),
);
const outputDirPath = fileURLToPath(new URL("../generated", import.meta.url));
const outputHtmlPath = fileURLToPath(
  new URL("../generated/index.html", import.meta.url),
);

async function bundleScript(): Promise<string> {
  const buildOutput = await build({
    entryPoints: [sourceScriptPath],
    bundle: true,
    format: "iife",
    globalName: "RandomPickerApp",
    platform: "browser",
    target: ["es2020"],
    write: false,
    outfile: "script.js",
  });

  const outputFile = buildOutput.outputFiles.find((file) =>
    file.path.endsWith(".js"),
  );
  if (!outputFile) {
    throw new Error("script bundle output not found");
  }

  return outputFile.text;
}

async function bundleStyle(): Promise<string> {
  const buildOutput = await build({
    entryPoints: [sourceCssPath],
    bundle: true,
    write: false,
    outfile: "style.css",
  });

  const outputFile = buildOutput.outputFiles.find((file) =>
    file.path.endsWith(".css"),
  );
  if (!outputFile) {
    throw new Error("style bundle output not found");
  }

  return outputFile.text;
}

function inlineTemplate(
  template: string,
  styleText: string,
  scriptText: string,
): string {
  const escapedScript = scriptText.replace(/<\/script>/g, "<\\/script>");
  const bootScript = `${escapedScript}\nRandomPickerApp.initApp();`;

  return template
    .replace("/* __INLINE_STYLE__ */", styleText)
    .replace("/* __INLINE_SCRIPT__ */", bootScript);
}

async function main(): Promise<void> {
  const template = fs.readFileSync(sourceHtmlPath, "utf8");
  const styleText = await bundleStyle();
  const scriptText = await bundleScript();
  const outputHtml = inlineTemplate(template, styleText, scriptText);
  const formattedHtml = await prettier.format(outputHtml, { parser: "html" });

  fs.mkdirSync(outputDirPath, { recursive: true });
  fs.writeFileSync(outputHtmlPath, formattedHtml, "utf8");
}

main().catch((error) => {
  console.error(error);
  process.exitCode = 1;
});

    <script>
      "use strict";
      var RandomPickerApp = (() => {
        var __defProp = Object.defineProperty;
        var __getOwnPropDesc = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor;
        var __getOwnPropNames = Object.getOwnPropertyNames;
        var __hasOwnProp = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty;
        var __export = (target, all) => {
          for (var name in all)
            __defProp(target, name, { get: all[name], enumerable: true });
        };
        var __copyProps = (to, from, except, desc) => {
          if (
            (from && typeof from === "object") ||
            typeof from === "function"
          ) {
            for (let key of __getOwnPropNames(from))
              if (!__hasOwnProp.call(to, key) && key !== except)
                __defProp(to, key, {
                  get: () => from[key],
                  enumerable:
                    !(desc = __getOwnPropDesc(from, key)) || desc.enumerable,
                });
          }
          return to;
        };
        var __toCommonJS = (mod) =>
          __copyProps(__defProp({}, "__esModule", { value: true }), mod);

        // apps/random-picker/src/script.ts
        var script_exports = {};
        __export(script_exports, {
          initApp: () => initApp,
        });

        // apps/random-picker/src/dom.ts
        function buildProcessorSelectOptions(selectEl, registry) {
          const sortedKeys = Object.keys(registry).sort();
          selectEl.innerHTML = "";
          sortedKeys.forEach((key) => {
            const def = registry[key];
            const option = document.createElement("option");
            option.value = def.id;
            option.textContent = def.name;
            selectEl.appendChild(option);
          });
        }
        function createUi(root = document) {
          return {
            inputCopyBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "inputCopyBtn"),
            inputOpenBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "inputOpenBtn"),
            input: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "input"),
            pipelineStepList: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "pipelineStepList"),
            processorSelect: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "processorSelect"),
            addStepBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "addStepBtn"),
            pipelineRunBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "pipelineRunBtn"),
            outputCopyBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "outputCopyBtn"),
            outputOpenBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "outputOpenBtn"),
            output: getElementByIdOrThrow(root, "output"),
          };
        }
        function getElementByIdOrThrow(root, id) {
          const element = root.getElementById(id);
          if (!element) {
            throw new Error(`Element not found: #${id}`);
          }
          return element;
        }
        function renderOutput(element, value) {
          element.value = value;
        }
        function renderPipelineStepList(listEl, steps, registry) {
          listEl.innerHTML = "";
          if (steps.length === 0) {
            const emptyMsg = document.createElement("div");
            emptyMsg.className = "pipeline-empty-msg";
            emptyMsg.textContent =
              "\u30B9\u30C6\u30C3\u30D7\u304C\u3042\u308A\u307E\u305B\u3093\u3002\u8FFD\u52A0\u3057\u3066\u304F\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002";
            listEl.appendChild(emptyMsg);
            return;
          }
          steps.forEach((step, index) => {
            const def = registry[step.id];
            if (!def) return;
            const item = document.createElement("div");
            item.className = "pipeline-step-item";
            item.draggable = true;
            item.dataset.index = index.toString();
            const handle = document.createElement("div");
            handle.className = "pipeline-drag-handle";
            handle.innerHTML =
              '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M5 9h14M5 15h14"/></svg>';
            item.appendChild(handle);
            const name = document.createElement("span");
            name.className = "pipeline-step-name";
            name.textContent = def.name;
            item.appendChild(name);
            const paramsContainer = document.createElement("div");
            paramsContainer.className = "pipeline-step-params";
            if (def.paramsSchema) {
              Object.entries(def.paramsSchema).forEach(([key, schema]) => {
                const span = document.createElement("span");
                span.textContent = schema.label;
                paramsContainer.appendChild(span);
                const input = document.createElement("input");
                input.type = schema.type === "number" ? "number" : "text";
                input.value = (step.params?.[key] ?? schema.default).toString();
                input.dataset.index = index.toString();
                input.dataset.key = key;
                paramsContainer.appendChild(input);
              });
            }
            item.appendChild(paramsContainer);
            const deleteBtn = document.createElement("button");
            deleteBtn.className = "pipeline-delete-btn";
            deleteBtn.type = "button";
            deleteBtn.dataset.index = index.toString();
            deleteBtn.innerHTML =
              '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M3 6h18M19 6v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H7a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6m3 0V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v2"/></svg>';
            item.appendChild(deleteBtn);
            listEl.appendChild(item);
          });
        }

        // apps/random-picker/src/browser.ts
        async function copyTextToClipboard(value) {
          await navigator.clipboard.writeText(value);
        }
        function openUrls(urls) {
          urls.forEach((url) => {
            window.open(url, "_blank");
          });
        }

        // apps/random-picker/src/pipeline.ts
        function addPipelineStep(steps, newStep) {
          return [...steps, newStep];
        }
        function applyStringArrayProcessors(items, processors) {
          return processors.reduce(
            (currentItems, processor) => processor(currentItems),
            items,
          );
        }
        function executePipeline(inputText, steps, context, processorRegistry) {
          let currentItems = splitByNewline(inputText);
          for (const step of steps) {
            const def = processorRegistry[step.id];
            if (!def) continue;
            const params = resolveParams(def, step.params);
            currentItems = def.execute(currentItems, params, context);
          }
          return joinByNewline(currentItems);
        }
        function joinByNewline(items) {
          return items.join("\n");
        }
        function movePipelineStep(steps, fromIndex, toIndex) {
          const newSteps = [...steps];
          if (!Number.isInteger(fromIndex) || !Number.isInteger(toIndex)) {
            return newSteps;
          }
          if (
            fromIndex < 0 ||
            toIndex < 0 ||
            fromIndex >= newSteps.length ||
            toIndex >= newSteps.length
          ) {
            return newSteps;
          }
          if (fromIndex === toIndex) {
            return newSteps;
          }
          const [removed] = newSteps.splice(fromIndex, 1);
          newSteps.splice(toIndex, 0, removed);
          return newSteps;
        }
        function removePipelineStep(steps, index) {
          return steps.filter((_, i) => i !== index);
        }
        function resolveParams(def, stepParams) {
          const defaults = {};
          if (def.paramsSchema) {
            for (const [key, field] of Object.entries(def.paramsSchema)) {
              defaults[key] = field.default;
            }
          }
          return { ...defaults, ...stepParams };
        }
        function splitByNewline(sourceText) {
          return sourceText.split("\n");
        }
        function updatePipelineStepParam(steps, index, key, value) {
          return steps.map((step, i) => {
            if (i !== index) return step;
            return {
              ...step,
              params: {
                ...(step.params ?? {}),
                [key]: value,
              },
            };
          });
        }

        // apps/random-picker/src/processor.ts
        function filterEmptyStrings(items) {
          return items.filter((item) => item !== "");
        }
        function pickRandomItems(items, count) {
          if (!Number.isSafeInteger(count) || count < 0) {
            throw new RangeError("count must be a non-negative safe integer");
          }
          const pickedCount = Math.min(count, items.length);
          const allIndexes = items.map((_, itemIndex) => itemIndex);
          for (
            let currentIndex = 0;
            currentIndex < pickedCount;
            currentIndex += 1
          ) {
            const randomIndex =
              currentIndex +
              Math.floor(Math.random() * (allIndexes.length - currentIndex));
            [allIndexes[currentIndex], allIndexes[randomIndex]] = [
              allIndexes[randomIndex],
              allIndexes[currentIndex],
            ];
          }
          const pickedIndexes = allIndexes
            .slice(0, pickedCount)
            .sort((left, right) => {
              return left - right;
            });
          return pickedIndexes.map((itemIndex) => items[itemIndex]);
        }
        function removeExcludedItems(items, excludedItems) {
          const excludedItemSet = new Set(excludedItems);
          return items.filter((item) => !excludedItemSet.has(item));
        }
        function trimStrings(items) {
          return items.map((item) => item.trim());
        }

        // apps/random-picker/src/event.ts
        function bindInputEvent(deps) {
          deps.ui.inputCopyBtn.onclick = async () => {
            await handleInputCopyBtnClick(deps);
          };
          deps.ui.inputOpenBtn.onclick = () => {
            handleInputOpenBtnClick(deps);
          };
        }
        function bindPipelineEvent(deps) {
          let draggingIndex = null;
          deps.ui.pipelineStepList.onclick = (event) => {
            handlePipelineStepListClick(deps, event);
          };
          deps.ui.pipelineStepList.ondragend = (event) => {
            handlePipelineStepListDragEnd(deps, event, (value) => {
              draggingIndex = value;
            });
          };
          deps.ui.pipelineStepList.ondragover = (event) => {
            handlePipelineStepListDragOver(
              deps,
              event,
              draggingIndex,
              (value) => {
                draggingIndex = value;
              },
            );
          };
          deps.ui.pipelineStepList.ondragstart = (event) => {
            handlePipelineStepListDragStart(deps, event, (value) => {
              draggingIndex = value;
            });
          };
          deps.ui.pipelineStepList.oninput = (event) => {
            handlePipelineStepListInput(deps, event);
          };
          deps.ui.addStepBtn.onclick = () => {
            handleAddStepBtnClick(deps);
          };
          deps.ui.pipelineRunBtn.onclick = () => {
            handlePipelineRunBtnClick(deps);
          };
        }
        function bindOutputEvent(deps) {
          deps.ui.outputCopyBtn.onclick = async () => {
            await handleOutputCopyBtnClick(deps);
          };
          deps.ui.outputOpenBtn.onclick = () => {
            handleOutputOpenBtnClick(deps);
          };
        }
        async function handleInputCopyBtnClick(deps) {
          const inputText = deps.ui.input.value;
          await copyTextToClipboard(inputText);
        }
        function handleInputOpenBtnClick(deps) {
          const inputText = deps.ui.input.value;
          const inputLines = splitByNewline(inputText);
          const urls = applyStringArrayProcessors(inputLines, [
            trimStrings,
            filterEmptyStrings,
          ]);
          openUrls(urls);
        }
        function handlePipelineStepListClick(deps, event) {
          const target = event.target;
          const deleteBtn = target.closest(".pipeline-delete-btn");
          if (deleteBtn) {
            const index = parseInt(deleteBtn.dataset.index ?? "-1", 10);
            if (index >= 0) {
              deps.appState.pipeline = removePipelineStep(
                deps.appState.pipeline,
                index,
              );
              renderPipelineStepList(
                deps.ui.pipelineStepList,
                deps.appState.pipeline,
                deps.processorRegistry,
              );
            }
          }
        }
        function handlePipelineStepListDragEnd(_deps, event, setDraggingIndex) {
          const target = event.target;
          const item = target.closest(".pipeline-step-item");
          if (item) {
            item.classList.remove("dragging");
          }
          setDraggingIndex(null);
        }
        function handlePipelineStepListDragOver(
          deps,
          event,
          draggingIndex,
          setDraggingIndex,
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          const target = event.target;
          const overItem = target.closest(".pipeline-step-item");
          if (overItem && draggingIndex !== null) {
            const overIndex = parseInt(overItem.dataset.index ?? "-1", 10);
            if (overIndex !== draggingIndex) {
              deps.appState.pipeline = movePipelineStep(
                deps.appState.pipeline,
                draggingIndex,
                overIndex,
              );
              setDraggingIndex(overIndex);
              renderPipelineStepList(
                deps.ui.pipelineStepList,
                deps.appState.pipeline,
                deps.processorRegistry,
              );
            }
          }
        }
        function handlePipelineStepListDragStart(
          _deps,
          event,
          setDraggingIndex,
        ) {
          const target = event.target;
          const item = target.closest(".pipeline-step-item");
          if (item) {
            setDraggingIndex(parseInt(item.dataset.index ?? "-1", 10));
            item.classList.add("dragging");
            if (event.dataTransfer) {
              event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = "move";
            }
          }
        }
        function handlePipelineStepListInput(deps, event) {
          const target = event.target;
          if (
            target.tagName === "INPUT" &&
            target.dataset.index &&
            target.dataset.key
          ) {
            const index = parseInt(target.dataset.index, 10);
            const key = target.dataset.key;
            const value =
              target.type === "number"
                ? parseFloat(target.value)
                : target.value;
            deps.appState.pipeline = updatePipelineStepParam(
              deps.appState.pipeline,
              index,
              key,
              value,
            );
          }
        }
        function handleAddStepBtnClick(deps) {
          const processorId = deps.ui.processorSelect.value;
          const def = deps.processorRegistry[processorId];
          if (!def) return;
          deps.appState.pipeline = addPipelineStep(deps.appState.pipeline, {
            id: processorId,
          });
          renderPipelineStepList(
            deps.ui.pipelineStepList,
            deps.appState.pipeline,
            deps.processorRegistry,
          );
        }
        function handlePipelineRunBtnClick(deps) {
          const inputText = deps.ui.input.value;
          const context = {
            previousOutput: deps.ui.output.value ?? "",
          };
          const outputText = executePipeline(
            inputText,
            deps.appState.pipeline,
            context,
            deps.processorRegistry,
          );
          renderOutput(deps.ui.output, outputText);
        }
        async function handleOutputCopyBtnClick(deps) {
          const outputText = deps.ui.output.value ?? "";
          await copyTextToClipboard(outputText);
        }
        function handleOutputOpenBtnClick(deps) {
          const outputText = deps.ui.output.value ?? "";
          const outputLines = splitByNewline(outputText);
          const urls = applyStringArrayProcessors(outputLines, [
            trimStrings,
            filterEmptyStrings,
          ]);
          openUrls(urls);
        }

        // apps/random-picker/src/processor-registry.ts
        var PROCESSOR_REGISTRY = {
          excludePrevious: {
            id: "excludePrevious",
            name: "\u524D\u56DE\u51FA\u529B\u3092\u9664\u5916",
            description:
              "\u524D\u56DE\u306E\u51FA\u529B\u7D50\u679C\u306B\u542B\u307E\u308C\u308B\u9805\u76EE\u3092\u9664\u5916\u3057\u307E\u3059",
            execute: (items, _params, context) =>
              removeExcludedItems(
                items,
                splitByNewline(context.previousOutput),
              ),
          },
          filterEmpty: {
            id: "filterEmpty",
            name: "\u7A7A\u884C\u9664\u5916",
            description:
              "\u7A7A\u306E\u884C\u3092\u9664\u5916\u3057\u307E\u3059",
            execute: (items) => filterEmptyStrings(items),
          },
          pickRandom: {
            id: "pickRandom",
            name: "\u30E9\u30F3\u30C0\u30E0\u62BD\u51FA",
            description:
              "\u6307\u5B9A\u3057\u305F\u4EF6\u6570\u3060\u3051\u30E9\u30F3\u30C0\u30E0\u306B\u9078\u3073\u307E\u3059",
            paramsSchema: {
              count: {
                type: "number",
                label: "\u62BD\u51FA\u4EF6\u6570",
                default: 1,
              },
            },
            execute: (items, params) => pickRandomItems(items, params["count"]),
          },
          trim: {
            id: "trim",
            name: "\u7A7A\u767D\u524A\u9664",
            description:
              "\u5404\u884C\u306E\u524D\u5F8C\u306E\u7A7A\u767D\u3092\u524A\u9664\u3057\u307E\u3059",
            execute: (items) => trimStrings(items),
          },
        };

        // apps/random-picker/src/state.ts
        var appState = {
          pipeline: [],
        };

        // apps/random-picker/src/script.ts
        function initApp(ui = createUi()) {
          appState.pipeline = [];
          buildProcessorSelectOptions(ui.processorSelect, PROCESSOR_REGISTRY);
          renderPipelineStepList(
            ui.pipelineStepList,
            appState.pipeline,
            PROCESSOR_REGISTRY,
          );
          const deps = { ui, appState, processorRegistry: PROCESSOR_REGISTRY };
          bindInputEvent(deps);
          bindPipelineEvent(deps);
          bindOutputEvent(deps);
          return ui;
        }
        return __toCommonJS(script_exports);
      })();

      RandomPickerApp.initApp();
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

FILE: apps/random-picker/src/browser.ts

/**
 * гғҶгӮӯгӮ№гғҲгӮ’гӮҜгғӘгғғгғ—гғңгғјгғүгҒ«гӮігғ”гғјгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export async function copyTextToClipboard(value: string): Promise<void> {
  await navigator.clipboard.writeText(value);
}

/**
 * URL й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’ж–°гҒ—гҒ„гӮҝгғ–гҒ§й ҶгҒ«й–ӢгҒҸ
 */
export function openUrls(urls: string[]): void {
  urls.forEach((url) => {
    window.open(url, "_blank");
  });
}



================================================
FILE: apps/random-picker/src/dom.ts
================================================
import type { PipelineStep, ProcessorDef, UI } from "./type.ts";

/**
 * PROCESSOR_REGISTRY гҒӢгӮүгӮ»гғ¬гӮҜгғҲгғңгғғгӮҜгӮ№гҒ®гӮӘгғ—гӮ·гғ§гғігӮ’ж§ӢзҜүгҒ—гҒҰиЁӯе®ҡгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function buildProcessorSelectOptions(
  selectEl: HTMLSelectElement,
  registry: Record<string, ProcessorDef>,
): void {
  const sortedKeys = Object.keys(registry).sort();
  selectEl.innerHTML = "";
  sortedKeys.forEach((key) => {
    const def = registry[key];
    const option = document.createElement("option");
    option.value = def.id;
    option.textContent = def.name;
    selectEl.appendChild(option);
  });
}

/**
 * UI иҰҒзҙ гӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function createUi(root: Document = document): UI {
  return {
    inputCopyBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLButtonElement>(
      root,
      "inputCopyBtn",
    ),
    inputOpenBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLButtonElement>(
      root,
      "inputOpenBtn",
    ),
    input: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLTextAreaElement>(root, "input"),
    pipelineStepList: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLElement>(
      root,
      "pipelineStepList",
    ),
    processorSelect: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLSelectElement>(
      root,
      "processorSelect",
    ),
    addStepBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLButtonElement>(root, "addStepBtn"),
    pipelineRunBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLButtonElement>(
      root,
      "pipelineRunBtn",
    ),
    outputCopyBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLButtonElement>(
      root,
      "outputCopyBtn",
    ),
    outputOpenBtn: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLButtonElement>(
      root,
      "outputOpenBtn",
    ),
    output: getElementByIdOrThrow<HTMLTextAreaElement>(root, "output"),
  };
}

/**
 * жҢҮе®ҡгҒ—гҒҹ ID гҒ®иҰҒзҙ гӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒ—гҖҒиҰӢгҒӨгҒӢгӮүгҒӘгҒ„е ҙеҗҲгҒҜдҫӢеӨ–гҒ«гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function getElementByIdOrThrow<T extends HTMLElement>(
  root: Document,
  id: string,
): T {
  const element = root.getElementById(id);
  if (!element) {
    throw new Error(`Element not found: #${id}`);
  }

  return element as T;
}

/**
 * з”»йқўгҒ«еҮәеҠӣгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function renderOutput(
  element: HTMLTextAreaElement,
  value: string,
): void {
  element.value = value;
}

/**
 * appState.pipeline гӮ’иӘӯгӮ“гҒ§гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—дёҖиҰ§гҒ®DOMгӮ’еҶҚжҸҸз”»гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function renderPipelineStepList(
  listEl: HTMLElement,
  steps: PipelineStep[],
  registry: Record<string, ProcessorDef>,
): void {
  listEl.innerHTML = "";

  if (steps.length === 0) {
    const emptyMsg = document.createElement("div");
    emptyMsg.className = "pipeline-empty-msg";
    emptyMsg.textContent = "гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гҒҢгҒӮгӮҠгҒҫгҒӣгӮ“гҖӮиҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰгҒҸгҒ гҒ•гҒ„гҖӮ";
    listEl.appendChild(emptyMsg);
    return;
  }

  steps.forEach((step, index) => {
    const def = registry[step.id];
    if (!def) return;

    const item = document.createElement("div");
    item.className = "pipeline-step-item";
    item.draggable = true;
    item.dataset.index = index.toString();

    // гғүгғ©гғғгӮ°гғҸгғігғүгғ«
    const handle = document.createElement("div");
    handle.className = "pipeline-drag-handle";
    handle.innerHTML =
      '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M5 9h14M5 15h14"/></svg>';
    item.appendChild(handle);

    // еҗҚеүҚ
    const name = document.createElement("span");
    name.className = "pipeline-step-name";
    name.textContent = def.name;
    item.appendChild(name);

    // гғ‘гғ©гғЎгғјгӮҝ
    const paramsContainer = document.createElement("div");
    paramsContainer.className = "pipeline-step-params";
    if (def.paramsSchema) {
      Object.entries(def.paramsSchema).forEach(([key, schema]) => {
        const span = document.createElement("span");
        span.textContent = schema.label;
        paramsContainer.appendChild(span);

        const input = document.createElement("input");
        input.type = schema.type === "number" ? "number" : "text";
        input.value = (step.params?.[key] ?? schema.default).toString();
        input.dataset.index = index.toString();
        input.dataset.key = key;
        paramsContainer.appendChild(input);
      });
    }
    item.appendChild(paramsContainer);

    // еүҠйҷӨгғңгӮҝгғі
    const deleteBtn = document.createElement("button");
    deleteBtn.className = "pipeline-delete-btn";
    deleteBtn.type = "button";
    deleteBtn.dataset.index = index.toString();
    deleteBtn.innerHTML =
      '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M3 6h18M19 6v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H7a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6m3 0V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v2"/></svg>';
    item.appendChild(deleteBtn);

    listEl.appendChild(item);
  });
}



================================================
FILE: apps/random-picker/src/event.ts
================================================
import type { EventDeps, PipelineContext } from "./type.ts";
import { copyTextToClipboard, openUrls } from "./browser.ts";
import { renderOutput, renderPipelineStepList } from "./dom.ts";
import {
  addPipelineStep,
  applyStringArrayProcessors,
  executePipeline,
  movePipelineStep,
  removePipelineStep,
  splitByNewline,
  updatePipelineStepParam,
} from "./pipeline.ts";
import { filterEmptyStrings, trimStrings } from "./processor.ts";

/**
 * е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гҒҫгӮҸгӮҠгҒ®гӮӨгғҷгғігғҲгӮ’зөҗз·ҡгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function bindInputEvent(deps: EventDeps): void {
  deps.ui.inputCopyBtn.onclick = async () => {
    await handleInputCopyBtnClick(deps);
  };

  deps.ui.inputOpenBtn.onclick = () => {
    handleInputOpenBtnClick(deps);
  };
}

/**
 * гғ‘гӮӨгғ—гғ©гӮӨгғігҒҫгӮҸгӮҠгҒ®гӮӨгғҷгғігғҲгӮ’зөҗз·ҡгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function bindPipelineEvent(deps: EventDeps): void {
  let draggingIndex: number | null = null;

  deps.ui.pipelineStepList.onclick = (event) => {
    handlePipelineStepListClick(deps, event);
  };

  deps.ui.pipelineStepList.ondragend = (event) => {
    handlePipelineStepListDragEnd(deps, event, (value) => {
      draggingIndex = value;
    });
  };

  deps.ui.pipelineStepList.ondragover = (event) => {
    handlePipelineStepListDragOver(deps, event, draggingIndex, (value) => {
      draggingIndex = value;
    });
  };

  deps.ui.pipelineStepList.ondragstart = (event) => {
    handlePipelineStepListDragStart(deps, event, (value) => {
      draggingIndex = value;
    });
  };

  deps.ui.pipelineStepList.oninput = (event) => {
    handlePipelineStepListInput(deps, event);
  };

  deps.ui.addStepBtn.onclick = () => {
    handleAddStepBtnClick(deps);
  };

  deps.ui.pipelineRunBtn.onclick = () => {
    handlePipelineRunBtnClick(deps);
  };
}

/**
 * еҮәеҠӣж¬„гҒҫгӮҸгӮҠгҒ®гӮӨгғҷгғігғҲгӮ’зөҗз·ҡгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function bindOutputEvent(deps: EventDeps): void {
  deps.ui.outputCopyBtn.onclick = async () => {
    await handleOutputCopyBtnClick(deps);
  };

  deps.ui.outputOpenBtn.onclick = () => {
    handleOutputOpenBtnClick(deps);
  };
}

/**
 * е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гҒ®гӮігғ”гғјгғңгӮҝгғіжҠјдёӢжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
async function handleInputCopyBtnClick(deps: EventDeps): Promise<void> {
  // е…ҘеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒҷгӮӢ
  const inputText = deps.ui.input.value;

  // е…ҘеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’гӮігғ”гғјгҒҷгӮӢ
  await copyTextToClipboard(inputText);
}

/**
 * е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гҒ®URLгӮӘгғјгғ—гғігғңгӮҝгғіжҠјдёӢжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handleInputOpenBtnClick(deps: EventDeps): void {
  // е…ҘеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒҷгӮӢ
  const inputText = deps.ui.input.value;

  // е…ҘеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’е…ҘеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гҒ«еҲҶеүІгҒҷгӮӢ
  const inputLines = splitByNewline(inputText);

  // е…ҘеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’ URL й…ҚеҲ—гҒ«еӨүжҸӣгҒҷгӮӢ
  const urls = applyStringArrayProcessors(inputLines, [
    trimStrings,
    filterEmptyStrings,
  ]);

  // URL й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’й–ӢгҒҸ
  openUrls(urls);
}

/**
 * гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—дёҖиҰ§гӮҜгғӘгғғгӮҜжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handlePipelineStepListClick(deps: EventDeps, event: MouseEvent): void {
  const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
  const deleteBtn = target.closest(".pipeline-delete-btn") as HTMLElement;
  if (deleteBtn) {
    const index = parseInt(deleteBtn.dataset.index ?? "-1", 10);
    if (index >= 0) {
      deps.appState.pipeline = removePipelineStep(
        deps.appState.pipeline,
        index,
      );
      renderPipelineStepList(
        deps.ui.pipelineStepList,
        deps.appState.pipeline,
        deps.processorRegistry,
      );
    }
  }
}

/**
 * гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—дёҖиҰ§гғүгғ©гғғгӮ°зөӮдәҶжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handlePipelineStepListDragEnd(
  _deps: EventDeps,
  event: DragEvent,
  setDraggingIndex: (value: number | null) => void,
): void {
  const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
  const item = target.closest(".pipeline-step-item") as HTMLElement;
  if (item) {
    item.classList.remove("dragging");
  }
  setDraggingIndex(null);
}

/**
 * гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—дёҖиҰ§гғүгғ©гғғгӮ°дёӯгҒ®йҮҚгҒӘгӮҠжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handlePipelineStepListDragOver(
  deps: EventDeps,
  event: DragEvent,
  draggingIndex: number | null,
  setDraggingIndex: (value: number) => void,
): void {
  event.preventDefault();
  const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
  const overItem = target.closest(".pipeline-step-item") as HTMLElement;
  if (overItem && draggingIndex !== null) {
    const overIndex = parseInt(overItem.dataset.index ?? "-1", 10);
    if (overIndex !== draggingIndex) {
      deps.appState.pipeline = movePipelineStep(
        deps.appState.pipeline,
        draggingIndex,
        overIndex,
      );
      setDraggingIndex(overIndex);
      renderPipelineStepList(
        deps.ui.pipelineStepList,
        deps.appState.pipeline,
        deps.processorRegistry,
      );
    }
  }
}

/**
 * гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—дёҖиҰ§гғүгғ©гғғгӮ°й–Ӣе§ӢжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handlePipelineStepListDragStart(
  _deps: EventDeps,
  event: DragEvent,
  setDraggingIndex: (value: number) => void,
): void {
  const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
  const item = target.closest(".pipeline-step-item") as HTMLElement;
  if (item) {
    setDraggingIndex(parseInt(item.dataset.index ?? "-1", 10));
    item.classList.add("dragging");
    if (event.dataTransfer) {
      event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = "move";
    }
  }
}

/**
 * гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—дёҖиҰ§е…ҘеҠӣеӨүжӣҙжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handlePipelineStepListInput(deps: EventDeps, event: Event): void {
  const target = event.target as HTMLInputElement;
  if (
    target.tagName === "INPUT" &&
    target.dataset.index &&
    target.dataset.key
  ) {
    const index = parseInt(target.dataset.index, 10);
    const key = target.dataset.key;
    const value =
      target.type === "number" ? parseFloat(target.value) : target.value;
    deps.appState.pipeline = updatePipelineStepParam(
      deps.appState.pipeline,
      index,
      key,
      value,
    );
  }
}

/**
 * гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—иҝҪеҠ гғңгӮҝгғіжҠјдёӢжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handleAddStepBtnClick(deps: EventDeps): void {
  const processorId = deps.ui.processorSelect.value;
  const def = deps.processorRegistry[processorId];
  if (!def) return;

  deps.appState.pipeline = addPipelineStep(deps.appState.pipeline, {
    id: processorId,
  });
  renderPipelineStepList(
    deps.ui.pipelineStepList,
    deps.appState.pipeline,
    deps.processorRegistry,
  );
}

/**
 * гғ‘гӮӨгғ—гғ©гӮӨгғіе®ҹиЎҢгғңгӮҝгғіжҠјдёӢжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handlePipelineRunBtnClick(deps: EventDeps): void {
  const inputText = deps.ui.input.value;
  const context: PipelineContext = {
    previousOutput: deps.ui.output.value ?? "",
  };
  const outputText = executePipeline(
    inputText,
    deps.appState.pipeline,
    context,
    deps.processorRegistry,
  );
  renderOutput(deps.ui.output, outputText);
}

/**
 * еҮәеҠӣж¬„гҒ®гӮігғ”гғјгғңгӮҝгғіжҠјдёӢжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
async function handleOutputCopyBtnClick(deps: EventDeps): Promise<void> {
  // еҮәеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒҷгӮӢ
  const outputText = deps.ui.output.value ?? "";

  // еҮәеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’гӮігғ”гғјгҒҷгӮӢ
  await copyTextToClipboard(outputText);
}

/**
 * еҮәеҠӣж¬„гҒ®URLгӮӘгғјгғ—гғігғңгӮҝгғіжҠјдёӢжҷӮгҒ®еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’иЎҢгҒҶ
 */
function handleOutputOpenBtnClick(deps: EventDeps): void {
  // еҮәеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒҷгӮӢ
  const outputText = deps.ui.output.value ?? "";

  // еҮәеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’еҮәеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гҒ«еҲҶеүІгҒҷгӮӢ
  const outputLines = splitByNewline(outputText);

  // еҮәеҠӣж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’ URL й…ҚеҲ—гҒ«еӨүжҸӣгҒҷгӮӢ
  const urls = applyStringArrayProcessors(outputLines, [
    trimStrings,
    filterEmptyStrings,
  ]);

  // URL й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’й–ӢгҒҸ
  openUrls(urls);
}

          <!-- JSгҒ§еӢ•зҡ„гҒ«з”ҹжҲҗ -->

FILE: apps/random-picker/src/pipeline.ts
================================================
import type {
  PipelineContext,
  PipelineStep,
  ProcessorDef,
  ProcessorParams,
  ProcessorRegistry,
  StringArrayProcessor,
} from "./type.ts";

/**
 * appState.pipeline гҒ«1гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гӮ’жң«е°ҫиҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰиҝ”гҒҷпјҲе…ғгҒ®й…ҚеҲ—гҒҜеӨүжӣҙгҒ—гҒӘгҒ„пјү
 */
export function addPipelineStep(
  steps: PipelineStep[],
  newStep: PipelineStep,
): PipelineStep[] {
  return [...steps, newStep];
}

/**
 * ж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гҒ«еҮҰзҗҶй–ўж•°гӮ’й Ҷз•ӘгҒ«йҒ©з”ЁгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function applyStringArrayProcessors(
  items: string[],
  processors: StringArrayProcessor[],
): string[] {
  return processors.reduce(
    (currentItems, processor) => processor(currentItems),
    items,
  );
}

/**
 * гғ‘гӮӨгғ—гғ©гӮӨгғігӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гӮ’й Ҷз•ӘгҒ«е®ҹиЎҢгҒ—гҖҒеҮәеҠӣгғҶгӮӯгӮ№гғҲгӮ’иҝ”гҒҷ
 */
export function executePipeline(
  inputText: string,
  steps: PipelineStep[],
  context: PipelineContext,
  processorRegistry: ProcessorRegistry,
): string {
  let currentItems = splitByNewline(inputText);

  for (const step of steps) {
    const def = processorRegistry[step.id];
    if (!def) continue;
    const params = resolveParams(def, step.params);
    currentItems = def.execute(currentItems, params, context);
  }

  return joinByNewline(currentItems);
}

/**
 * ж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’ж”№иЎҢж–Үеӯ—гҒ§зөҗеҗҲгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function joinByNewline(items: string[]): string {
  return items.join("\n");
}

/**
 * appState.pipeline гҒ® fromIndex вҶ’ toIndex гҒёиҰҒзҙ гӮ’з§»еӢ•гҒ—гҒҰиҝ”гҒҷпјҲе…ғгҒ®й…ҚеҲ—гҒҜеӨүжӣҙгҒ—гҒӘгҒ„пјү
 */
export function movePipelineStep(
  steps: PipelineStep[],
  fromIndex: number,
  toIndex: number,
): PipelineStep[] {
  const newSteps = [...steps];

  if (!Number.isInteger(fromIndex) || !Number.isInteger(toIndex)) {
    return newSteps;
  }

  if (
    fromIndex < 0 ||
    toIndex < 0 ||
    fromIndex >= newSteps.length ||
    toIndex >= newSteps.length
  ) {
    return newSteps;
  }

  if (fromIndex === toIndex) {
    return newSteps;
  }

  const [removed] = newSteps.splice(fromIndex, 1);
  newSteps.splice(toIndex, 0, removed);

  return newSteps;
}

/**
 * appState.pipeline гҒ®жҢҮе®ҡгӮӨгғігғҮгғғгӮҜгӮ№гӮ’еүҠйҷӨгҒ—гҒҰиҝ”гҒҷпјҲе…ғгҒ®й…ҚеҲ—гҒҜеӨүжӣҙгҒ—гҒӘгҒ„пјү
 */
export function removePipelineStep(
  steps: PipelineStep[],
  index: number,
): PipelineStep[] {
  return steps.filter((_, i) => i !== index);
}

/**
 * paramsSchema гҒ®гғҮгғ•гӮ©гғ«гғҲеҖӨгӮ’еҹәжә–гҒ«гҖҒгӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гҒ® params гӮ’гғһгғјгӮёгҒ—гҒҰиҝ”гҒҷ
 */
export function resolveParams(
  def: ProcessorDef,
  stepParams?: ProcessorParams,
): ProcessorParams {
  const defaults: ProcessorParams = {};
  if (def.paramsSchema) {
    for (const [key, field] of Object.entries(def.paramsSchema)) {
      defaults[key] = field.default;
    }
  }
  return { ...defaults, ...stepParams };
}

/**
 * ж”№иЎҢгҒ§ж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’еҲҶеүІгҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function splitByNewline(sourceText: string): string[] {
  return sourceText.split("\n");
}

/**
 * жҢҮе®ҡгӮӨгғігғҮгғғгӮҜгӮ№гҒ®гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гҒ® params гӮ’жӣҙж–°гҒ—гҒҰиҝ”гҒҷпјҲе…ғгҒ®й…ҚеҲ—гҒҜеӨүжӣҙгҒ—гҒӘгҒ„пјү
 */
export function updatePipelineStepParam(
  steps: PipelineStep[],
  index: number,
  key: string,
  value: number | string,
): PipelineStep[] {
  return steps.map((step, i) => {
    if (i !== index) return step;
    return {
      ...step,
      params: {
        ...(step.params ?? {}),
        [key]: value,
      },
    };
  });
}

import type { ProcessorRegistry } from "./type.ts";
import { splitByNewline } from "./pipeline.ts";
import {
  filterEmptyStrings,
  pickRandomItems,
  removeExcludedItems,
  trimStrings,
} from "./processor.ts";

/** гғ—гғӯгӮ»гғғгӮөгҒ®зҷ»йҢІгғӘгӮ№гғҲ */
export const PROCESSOR_REGISTRY: ProcessorRegistry = {
  excludePrevious: {
    id: "excludePrevious",
    name: "еүҚеӣһеҮәеҠӣгӮ’йҷӨеӨ–",
    description: "еүҚеӣһгҒ®еҮәеҠӣзөҗжһңгҒ«еҗ«гҒҫгӮҢгӮӢй …зӣ®гӮ’йҷӨеӨ–гҒ—гҒҫгҒҷ",
    execute: (items, _params, context) =>
      removeExcludedItems(items, splitByNewline(context.previousOutput)),
  },
  filterEmpty: {
    id: "filterEmpty",
    name: "з©әиЎҢйҷӨеӨ–",
    description: "з©әгҒ®иЎҢгӮ’йҷӨеӨ–гҒ—гҒҫгҒҷ",
    execute: (items) => filterEmptyStrings(items),
  },
  pickRandom: {
    id: "pickRandom",
    name: "гғ©гғігғҖгғ жҠҪеҮә",
    description: "жҢҮе®ҡгҒ—гҒҹд»¶ж•°гҒ гҒ‘гғ©гғігғҖгғ гҒ«йҒёгҒігҒҫгҒҷ",
    paramsSchema: {
      count: { type: "number", label: "жҠҪеҮәд»¶ж•°", default: 1 },
    },
    execute: (items, params) =>
      pickRandomItems(items, params["count"] as number),
  },
  trim: {
    id: "trim",
    name: "з©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨ",
    description: "еҗ„иЎҢгҒ®еүҚеҫҢгҒ®з©әзҷҪгӮ’еүҠйҷӨгҒ—гҒҫгҒҷ",
    execute: (items) => trimStrings(items),
  },
};

FILE: apps/random-picker/src/processor.ts
================================================
/**
 * з©әж–Үеӯ—еҲ—гӮ’йҷӨеӨ–гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function filterEmptyStrings(items: string[]): string[] {
  return items.filter((item) => item !== "");
}

/**
 * й…ҚеҲ—гҒӢгӮүгғ©гғігғҖгғ гҒ«жҢҮе®ҡд»¶ж•°гҒ¶гӮ“йҒёгӮ“гҒ й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’иҝ”гҒҷ
 */
export function pickRandomItems(items: string[], count: number): string[] {
  if (!Number.isSafeInteger(count) || count < 0) {
    throw new RangeError("count must be a non-negative safe integer");
  }

  const pickedCount = Math.min(count, items.length);
  const allIndexes = items.map((_, itemIndex) => itemIndex);

  for (let currentIndex = 0; currentIndex < pickedCount; currentIndex += 1) {
    const randomIndex =
      currentIndex +
      Math.floor(Math.random() * (allIndexes.length - currentIndex));
    [allIndexes[currentIndex], allIndexes[randomIndex]] = [
      allIndexes[randomIndex],
      allIndexes[currentIndex],
    ];
  }

  const pickedIndexes = allIndexes.slice(0, pickedCount).sort((left, right) => {
    return left - right;
  });

  return pickedIndexes.map((itemIndex) => items[itemIndex]);
}

/**
 * йҷӨеӨ–гғӘгӮ№гғҲгӮ’йҒ©з”ЁгҒ—гҒҹй…ҚеҲ—гӮ’иҝ”гҒҷ
 */
export function removeExcludedItems(
  items: string[],
  excludedItems: string[],
): string[] {
  const excludedItemSet = new Set(excludedItems);
  return items.filter((item) => !excludedItemSet.has(item));
}

/**
 * ж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гҒ®еҗ„иҰҒзҙ гӮ’ trim гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function trimStrings(items: string[]): string[] {
  return items.map((item) => item.trim());
}



================================================
FILE: apps/random-picker/src/script.ts
================================================
import type { UI } from "./type.ts";
import {
  buildProcessorSelectOptions,
  createUi,
  renderPipelineStepList,
} from "./dom.ts";
import { bindInputEvent, bindOutputEvent, bindPipelineEvent } from "./event.ts";
import { PROCESSOR_REGISTRY } from "./processor-registry.ts";
import { appState } from "./state.ts";

/**
 * гӮўгғ—гғӘгӮ’еҲқжңҹеҢ–гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
export function initApp(ui: UI = createUi()): UI {
  appState.pipeline = [];

  buildProcessorSelectOptions(ui.processorSelect, PROCESSOR_REGISTRY);
  renderPipelineStepList(
    ui.pipelineStepList,
    appState.pipeline,
    PROCESSOR_REGISTRY,
  );

  const deps = { ui, appState, processorRegistry: PROCESSOR_REGISTRY };

  bindInputEvent(deps);
  bindPipelineEvent(deps);
  bindOutputEvent(deps);

  return ui;
}

export const appState: AppState = {
  pipeline: [],
};

FILE: apps/random-picker/src/type.ts
================================================
/** гӮўгғ—гғӘгӮұгғјгӮ·гғ§гғігҒ®зҠ¶ж…Ӣ */
export type AppState = {
  pipeline: PipelineStep[];
};

/** гӮӨгғҷгғігғҲзөҗз·ҡгҒ§еҸ—гҒ‘жёЎгҒҷдҫқеӯҳй–ўдҝӮ */
export type EventDeps = {
  ui: UI;
  appState: AppState;
  processorRegistry: ProcessorRegistry;
};

/** гғ‘гғ©гғЎгғјгӮҝгӮ№гӮӯгғјгғһгҒ®1гғ•гӮЈгғјгғ«гғүгҒ®е®ҡзҫ© */
export type ParamFieldSchema = {
  type: "number" | "string";
  label: string;
  default: number | string;
};

/** гғ‘гӮӨгғ—гғ©гӮӨгғіе®ҹиЎҢжҷӮгҒ«жёЎгҒҷе®ҹиЎҢгӮігғігғҶгӮӯгӮ№гғҲ */
export type PipelineContext = {
  /** жҺ’д»–гғ©гғігғҖгғ зӯүгҒ§еҸӮз…§гҒҷгӮӢеүҚеӣһгҒ®еҮәеҠӣгғҶгӮӯгӮ№гғҲпјҲж”№иЎҢеҢәеҲҮгӮҠпјү */
  previousOutput: string;
};

/** гғҰгғјгӮ¶гғјгҒҢзө„гҒҝз«ӢгҒҰгҒҹгғ‘гӮӨгғ—гғ©гӮӨгғігҒ®1гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ— */
export type PipelineStep = {
  id: string;
  params?: ProcessorParams;
};

/** гғ—гғӯгӮ»гғғгӮөгҒ®е®ҡзҫ©пјҲгғЎгӮҝгғҮгғјгӮҝпјӢе®ҹиЎҢгғӯгӮёгғғгӮҜпјү */
export type ProcessorDef = {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  paramsSchema?: Record<string, ParamFieldSchema>;
  execute: (
    items: string[],
    params: ProcessorParams,
    context: PipelineContext,
  ) => string[];
};

/** гғ—гғӯгӮ»гғғгӮөгҒҢеҸ—гҒ‘еҸ–гӮӢгғ‘гғ©гғЎгғјгӮҝгҒ®еһӢ */
export type ProcessorParams = Record<string, number | string>;

/** гғ—гғӯгӮ»гғғгӮөгҒ®зҷ»йҢІиЎЁ */
export type ProcessorRegistry = Record<string, ProcessorDef>;

/** ж–Үеӯ—еҲ—й…ҚеҲ—гӮ’еҸ—гҒ‘еҸ–гӮҠгҖҒеҠ е·ҘгҒ—гҒҰиҝ”гҒҷеҮҰзҗҶй–ўж•°гҒ®еһӢ */
export type StringArrayProcessor = (items: string[]) => string[];

export type UI = {
  inputCopyBtn: HTMLButtonElement;
  inputOpenBtn: HTMLButtonElement;
  input: HTMLTextAreaElement;
  pipelineStepList: HTMLElement;
  processorSelect: HTMLSelectElement;
  addStepBtn: HTMLButtonElement;
  pipelineRunBtn: HTMLButtonElement;
  outputCopyBtn: HTMLButtonElement;
  outputOpenBtn: HTMLButtonElement;
  output: HTMLTextAreaElement;
};

FILE: apps/random-picker/tests/e2e/e2e.spec.ts

import { expect, test, type Page } from "@playwright/test";

const appUrl = new URL("../../generated/index.html", import.meta.url).href;

type OpenedUrl = {
  url: string;
  target: string | undefined;
};

type RandomPickerTestWindow = Window & {
  __copiedTexts: string[];
  __openedUrls: OpenedUrl[];
};

/**
 * гғ–гғ©гӮҰгӮ¶ API гӮ’гғҶгӮ№гғҲз”ЁгӮ№гӮҝгғ–гҒ«е·®гҒ—жӣҝгҒҲгӮӢ
 */
async function installBrowserApiStubs(page: Page): Promise<void> {
  await page.addInitScript(() => {
    const testWindow = window as unknown as RandomPickerTestWindow;

    testWindow.__copiedTexts = [];
    testWindow.__openedUrls = [];

    Object.defineProperty(navigator, "clipboard", {
      configurable: true,
      value: {
        writeText(text: string): Promise<void> {
          testWindow.__copiedTexts.push(text);
          return Promise.resolve();
        },
      },
    });

    window.open = ((url?: string | URL, target?: string) => {
      testWindow.__openedUrls.push({ url: String(url ?? ""), target });
      return null;
    }) as Window["open"];
  });
}

/**
 * гӮігғ”гғјеұҘжӯҙгӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
function getCopiedTexts(page: Page): Promise<string[]> {
  return page.evaluate(() => {
    const testWindow = window as unknown as RandomPickerTestWindow;
    return testWindow.__copiedTexts;
  });
}

/**
 * ж–°гҒ—гҒ„гӮҝгғ–иө·еӢ•еұҘжӯҙгӮ’еҸ–еҫ—гҒҷгӮӢ
 */
function getOpenedUrls(page: Page): Promise<OpenedUrl[]> {
  return page.evaluate(() => {
    const testWindow = window as unknown as RandomPickerTestWindow;
    return testWindow.__openedUrls;
  });
}

test.describe("еҲқжңҹиЎЁзӨә", () => {
  test("01 дё»иҰҒиҰҒзҙ гҒЁеҲқжңҹзҠ¶ж…ӢгӮ’иЎЁзӨәгҒҷгӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    // дё»иҰҒиҰҒзҙ гҒ®еӯҳеңЁзўәиӘҚ
    await expect(page.locator("#input")).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator("#output")).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator("#processorSelect")).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator("#addStepBtn")).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator("#pipelineRunBtn")).toBeVisible();
    await expect(
      page.getByRole("button", { name: "е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гӮ’гӮігғ”гғј" }),
    ).toBeVisible();
    await expect(
      page.getByRole("button", { name: "е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гҒ®гғӘгғігӮҜгӮ’ж–°гҒ—гҒ„гӮҝгғ–гҒ§й–ӢгҒҸ" }),
    ).toBeVisible();
    await expect(
      page.getByRole("button", { name: "еҮәеҠӣж¬„гӮ’гӮігғ”гғј" }),
    ).toBeVisible();
    await expect(
      page.getByRole("button", { name: "еҮәеҠӣж¬„гҒ®гғӘгғігӮҜгӮ’ж–°гҒ—гҒ„гӮҝгғ–гҒ§й–ӢгҒҸ" }),
    ).toBeVisible();

    // еҲқжңҹеҖӨгҒ®зўәиӘҚ
    await expect(page.locator("#input")).toHaveValue("");
    await expect(page.locator("#output")).toHaveValue("");
    await expect(
      page.getByText("гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гҒҢгҒӮгӮҠгҒҫгҒӣгӮ“гҖӮиҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰгҒҸгҒ гҒ•гҒ„гҖӮ"),
    ).toBeVisible();
  });
});

test.describe("е…ҘеҠӣж¬„", () => {
  test("01 гӮігғ”гғјгғңгӮҝгғіпјҸе…ҘеҠӣеҶ…е®№гӮ’гӮігғ”гғјгҒ§гҒҚгӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await installBrowserApiStubs(page);
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    await page.locator("#input").fill("A\nB");
    await page.getByRole("button", { name: "е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гӮ’гӮігғ”гғј" }).click();

    await expect.poll(() => getCopiedTexts(page)).toEqual(["A\nB"]);
  });

  test("02 гӮӘгғјгғ—гғігғңгӮҝгғіпјҸе…ҘеҠӣеҶ…е®№гҒ®URLгӮ’й–ӢгҒ‘гӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await installBrowserApiStubs(page);
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    await page
      .locator("#input")
      .fill(" https://example.com \n\nhttps://example.org ");
    await page
      .getByRole("button", { name: "е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гҒ®гғӘгғігӮҜгӮ’ж–°гҒ—гҒ„гӮҝгғ–гҒ§й–ӢгҒҸ" })
      .click();

    await expect
      .poll(() => getOpenedUrls(page))
      .toEqual([
        { url: "https://example.com", target: "_blank" },
        { url: "https://example.org", target: "_blank" },
      ]);
  });
});

test.describe("гғ‘гӮӨгғ—гғ©гӮӨгғі", () => {
  test("01 иҝҪеҠ гғ»еүҠйҷӨпјҸгӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гӮ’иҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰеүҠйҷӨгҒ§гҒҚгӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    // trim гӮ’иҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰзўәиӘҚ
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("trim");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-item")).toHaveCount(1);
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-name")).toHaveText("з©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨ");

    // filterEmpty гӮ’иҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰзўәиӘҚ
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("filterEmpty");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-item")).toHaveCount(2);
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-name")).toHaveText([
      "з©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨ",
      "з©әиЎҢйҷӨеӨ–",
    ]);

    // 2д»¶зӣ®гӮ’еүҠйҷӨгҒ—гҒҰзўәиӘҚ
    await page
      .locator(".pipeline-step-item")
      .nth(1)
      .locator(".pipeline-delete-btn")
      .click();
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-item")).toHaveCount(1);
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-name")).toHaveText(["з©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨ"]);
  });

  test("02 дёҰгҒіжӣҝгҒҲпјҸгӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—й ҶгҒ®еӨүжӣҙгӮ’е®ҹиЎҢзөҗжһңгҒ«еҸҚжҳ гҒ§гҒҚгӮӢ", async ({
    page,
  }) => {
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    // trim вҶ’ filterEmpty гҒ®й ҶгҒ§иҝҪеҠ 
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("trim");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("filterEmpty");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-name")).toHaveText([
      "з©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨ",
      "з©әиЎҢйҷӨеӨ–",
    ]);

    // dragstart / dragover гҒ§1д»¶зӣ®гӮ’2д»¶зӣ®гҒ®дҪҚзҪ®гҒёз§»еӢ•
    const dataTransfer = await page.evaluateHandle(() => new DataTransfer());
    await page
      .locator(".pipeline-step-item")
      .nth(0)
      .dispatchEvent("dragstart", { dataTransfer });
    await page
      .locator(".pipeline-step-item")
      .nth(1)
      .dispatchEvent("dragover", { dataTransfer });

    // дёҰгҒіжӣҝгҒҲеҫҢгҒ®й ҶеәҸгӮ’зўәиӘҚ
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-name")).toHaveText([
      "з©әиЎҢйҷӨеӨ–",
      "з©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨ",
    ]);

    // dragend гӮ’дёҰгҒіжӣҝгҒҲеҫҢ2д»¶зӣ®пјҲз©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨпјүгҒ« dispatch
    await page
      .locator(".pipeline-step-item")
      .nth(1)
      .dispatchEvent("dragend", { dataTransfer });

    // з©әиЎҢйҷӨеӨ– вҶ’ з©әзҷҪеүҠйҷӨ гҒ®й ҶгҒ§е®ҹиЎҢгҒҷгӮӢгҒЁ " \n A " вҶ’ "\nA" гҒ«гҒӘгӮӢ
    await page.locator("#input").fill(" \n A ");
    await page.locator("#pipelineRunBtn").click();
    await expect(page.locator("#output")).toHaveValue("\nA");
  });

  test("03 е®ҹиЎҢпјҸиҝҪеҠ гҒ®е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гҒҢгҒӘгҒҸгҖҒеҮәеҠӣж¬„гҒ®еҶ…е®№гӮ’дҪҝгӮҸгҒӘгҒ„еҮҰзҗҶгӮ’е®ҹиЎҢгҒ§гҒҚгӮӢ", async ({
    page,
  }) => {
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    // trim вҶ’ filterEmpty гӮ’иҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰе®ҹиЎҢ
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("trim");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("filterEmpty");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();

    await page.locator("#input").fill("  A  \n\n  B  \n  C  ");
    await page.locator("#pipelineRunBtn").click();

    await expect(page.locator("#output")).toHaveValue("A\nB\nC");
  });

  test("04 е®ҹиЎҢпјҸиҝҪеҠ гҒ®е…ҘеҠӣж¬„гҒҢгҒӮгӮӢеҮҰзҗҶгӮ’е®ҹиЎҢгҒ§гҒҚгӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    // pickRandom гӮ’иҝҪеҠ 
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("pickRandom");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();
    await expect(page.locator(".pipeline-step-item")).toHaveCount(1);

    // иҝҪеҠ е…ҘеҠӣж¬„пјҲжҠҪеҮәд»¶ж•°пјүгҒ®еӯҳеңЁгҒЁеҲқжңҹеҖӨгӮ’зўәиӘҚ
    const countInput = page
      .locator(".pipeline-step-item")
      .nth(0)
      .locator('input[type="number"]');
    await expect(countInput).toHaveCount(1);
    await expect(countInput).toHaveValue("1");

    // жҠҪеҮәд»¶ж•°гӮ’ 2 гҒ«еӨүжӣҙгҒ—гҒҰе®ҹиЎҢ
    await countInput.fill("2");
    await page.locator("#input").fill("A\nB\nC\nD");
    await page.locator("#pipelineRunBtn").click();

    // зөҗжһңгҒҜ A/B/C/D гҒӢгӮүйҮҚиӨҮгҒӘгҒ— 2 д»¶
    const result = await page.locator("#output").inputValue();
    const resultLines = result.split("\n").filter((l) => l.trim() !== "");
    expect(resultLines.length).toBe(2);
    for (const line of resultLines) {
      expect(["A", "B", "C", "D"]).toContain(line);
    }
    expect(new Set(resultLines).size).toBe(2);
  });

  test("05 е®ҹиЎҢпјҸеҮәеҠӣж¬„гҒ®еҶ…е®№гӮ’дҪҝгҒҶеҮҰзҗҶгӮ’е®ҹиЎҢгҒ§гҒҚгӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    // гӮ№гғҶгғғгғ—гҒӘгҒ—гҒ§е®ҹиЎҢгҒ—гҒҰеүҚеӣһеҮәеҠӣгӮ’дҪңгӮӢ
    await page.locator("#input").fill("A\nB\nC");
    await page.locator("#pipelineRunBtn").click();
    await expect(page.locator("#output")).toHaveValue("A\nB\nC");

    // excludePrevious гӮ’иҝҪеҠ гҒ—гҒҰеҶҚе®ҹиЎҢ
    await page.locator("#processorSelect").selectOption("excludePrevious");
    await page.locator("#addStepBtn").click();
    await page.locator("#input").fill("A\nB\nC\nD");
    await page.locator("#pipelineRunBtn").click();

    // еүҚеӣһеҮәеҠӣпјҲA/B/CпјүгӮ’йҷӨеӨ–гҒ—гҒҹ D гҒ гҒ‘гҒҢж®ӢгӮӢ
    await expect(page.locator("#output")).toHaveValue("D");
  });
});

test.describe("еҮәеҠӣж¬„", () => {
  test("01 гӮігғ”гғјгғңгӮҝгғіпјҸеҮәеҠӣеҶ…е®№гӮ’гӮігғ”гғјгҒ§гҒҚгӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await installBrowserApiStubs(page);
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    await page.locator("#output").evaluate((el) => {
      (el as HTMLTextAreaElement).value = "X\nY";
    });
    await page.getByRole("button", { name: "еҮәеҠӣж¬„гӮ’гӮігғ”гғј" }).click();

    await expect.poll(() => getCopiedTexts(page)).toEqual(["X\nY"]);
  });

  test("02 гӮӘгғјгғ—гғігғңгӮҝгғіпјҸеҮәеҠӣеҶ…е®№гҒ®URLгӮ’й–ӢгҒ‘гӮӢ", async ({ page }) => {
    await installBrowserApiStubs(page);
    await page.goto(appUrl);

    await page.locator("#output").evaluate((el) => {
      (el as HTMLTextAreaElement).value =
        " https://example.com/output \n\nhttps://example.org/output ";
    });
    await page
      .getByRole("button", { name: "еҮәеҠӣж¬„гҒ®гғӘгғігӮҜгӮ’ж–°гҒ—гҒ„гӮҝгғ–гҒ§й–ӢгҒҸ" })
      .click();

    await expect
      .poll(() => getOpenedUrls(page))
      .toEqual([
        { url: "https://example.com/output", target: "_blank" },
        { url: "https://example.org/output", target: "_blank" },
      ]);
  });
});
